1. The Chinese Communist publish in Peking, China, a magasine named
Crdina Reconstructs. This publication parallels other Communist publications
in its attacks on the United States, imperialism, etc.
2. Idem, who, it is believed, was of previous interest to HUSODA had
written for this magazine a highly ledatory article on the industrial and
agricultural progress made by the Chinese Communities during the preceding
year. Idem reportedly visited the Midland during the fall of 1950 and may
still be in that area.
3. The Jamuary 1959 issue of China Reconstructs carries the article
by Idem.

Soviet underground web was voven deep into Washington in the early New Deal days to

of talks with 'nittaker CHAMBERS, chief acensuer of HISS and former courier for a
Russian spy ring.
